Margin structure: Subscriptions and data licensing are high-margin (>80% gross margin once the platform is built — marginal cost of serving an additional subscriber is near-zero). Advisory services are lower margin (~50–60%) but build relationships that convert to subscription and licensing revenue. The business model is designed to shift from advisory-heavy in Year 1 to subscription/licensing-dominant by Year 3.
Section 6

Timeline & Milestones

Month 0 Project Kick-Off SSI v4.0 live. Dual BESS reference specifications (Config A: 4.9 MW / Config B: 9.9 MW) finalised. Data acquisition plan locked.
Months 1–4 Phase 1: BESS Value-Add Engine (Italy) Build DNO + Community value stacks for both Config A (4.9 MW) and Config B (9.9 MW). Produce dual-config Value-Add Cards for all 39,234 Italian substations. Internal validation complete.
Month 4 Milestone: Italian Value-Add Cards Published First commercial-grade output. Dual-config Value-Add Cards (Config A + Config B) for all 39,234 Italian substations. Advisory services can begin. SSI Monthly Intelligence incorporates BESS rankings.
Months 4–8 Phase 2: Real Options Pricing Model (Italy) Build TCO + Revenue Stack + Real Options for all Italian substations. Longstaff-Schwartz Monte Carlo operational.
Months 6–8 (parallel) Phase 3: Neural Network Training Train base model on Italian data. Feature reduction experiments. Transfer-learning architecture validated.
Month 8 Milestone: Italian Platform Complete Full value-add + real options + NN for Italy. Subscription platform launched. First paying subscribers.
Months 8–16 Phase 4 Tier 1: UK, Germany, France, Spain Full SSI-equivalent data acquisition + NN fine-tuning per country. UK first (deepest BESS market data for backtesting).
Month 12 Milestone: UK + Germany Live Two largest EU BESS markets covered. Backtesting against ~180 operational assets complete. Enterprise tier opens.
Months 14–22 Phase 4 Tier 2: NL, IE, BE, PL, GR, PT NN transfer-learning approach. Regulatory mapping per country. Advisory revenue from country-entry strategies.
Month 16 Milestone: All Tier 1 Countries Live 5 countries, ~300K substations. Data licensing conversations with BNEF/S&P begin. First Annual Retainer client.
Months 18–30 Phase 4 Tier 3: Remaining EU countries NN transfer-learning only. On-demand upgrade to full SSI for high-demand markets.
Month 24 Milestone: Full EU + UK Coverage 28 countries, ~500K substations. Platform is the most comprehensive open-access BESS valuation tool in Europe. Data licensing live.

Section 8

Risk Register

RiskImpactLikelihoodMitigation
Data access regression — a country restricts substation-level data that was previously publicHighLowNN transfer-learning is designed for this: the model degrades gracefully with partial data. Maintain multiple data source pipelines per country. Engage with Open Data initiatives (EU PSI Directive).
Capacity market design changes — a Tier 1 country closes or restructures its CM (e.g., UK reviews post-2030)MediumMediumRevenue stack model is modular: CM contribution can be toggled. Real options framework explicitly prices market design uncertainty via Option D (abandon). Scenario analysis in valuations covers CM abolition.
BESS cost trajectory faster/slower than assumed — disrupts TCO model and Option A (defer) valueMediumMediumMonte Carlo naturally captures this via stochastic cost path. Quarterly recalibration against BNEF cost survey. Faster cost decline increases platform value (more projects viable).
Competitor launches similar product — BNEF, Wood Mac, or a well-funded startupHighMediumSSI's substation-level granularity is the moat. Competitors would need to replicate the entire SSI v4.0 data pipeline per country. IP protection via USCO + SIAE deposits. First-mover advantage in institutional relationships (JRC, ACER). Academic validation network provides credibility barrier.
NN accuracy insufficient for Tier 2–3 countries — transfer learning fails to generaliseMediumLow–MediumUncertainty bounds widen automatically (quantile regression). Flag low-confidence predictions to users. Upgrade on-demand: if a Tier 3 country shows commercial traction, invest in full SSI-equivalent data acquisition.
Regulatory barrier to BESS deployment in a key market — e.g., planning moratoria, grid connection queue freezeMediumLowThe platform's value increases during regulatory uncertainty: developers need better intelligence precisely when market conditions are volatile. Regulatory Navigation advisory service directly monetises this.
Technology displacement — a non-BESS technology (e.g., hydrogen electrolysis, compressed air) becomes dominant for grid flexibilityMediumLow (within 30-yr horizon for existing BESS)Architecture is asset-agnostic at the engine level: swap the BESS TCO/revenue module for any flexibility asset. Long-term product evolution includes multi-technology comparison.
Section 9

IP Strategy

The SSI-ENN extends the IP protection framework established for the SSI v4.0. The following registrations and deposits cover the new work:

IP AssetProtection MechanismJurisdictionStatus
SSI-ENN Valuation Methodology (BESS Value-Add + Real Options)USCO registration (technical reference) + SIAE deposito opere inediteUS + Italy (dual jurisdiction)To be filed at Phase 2 completion
Neural Network Architecture & Training CodeUSCO registration (source code) + SIAE depositoUS + ItalyTo be filed at Phase 3 completion
Per-Country Regulatory MappingsSIAE deposito (database right under EU Directive 96/9/EC)Italy (EU-wide effect)To be filed per country as completed
Commercial Platform (code + design)USCO registration + SIAE depositoUS + ItalyTo be filed at Phase 5 launch
SSI-ENN TrademarkEUIPO registration (word mark + figurative mark)EU-wideTo be filed at Phase 5 launch
Existing SSI v4.0 IPUSCO triple registration + SIAE triple depositUS + ItalyCompleted
Database right (sui generis): The EU Database Directive 96/9/EC provides a 15-year right against extraction/re-utilisation of a substantial part of a database that required substantial investment to create. The SSI-ENN's per-substation valuation database for ~500K EU substations — built through systematic data acquisition, cleaning, modelling, and validation — qualifies for this protection. This is potentially the strongest IP protection for the dataset, independent of copyright.
